You may not bundle the list with any other product or service without prior written approval of the editor. In short, we give the list away for free, without any financial benefit, and we expect you to do likewise. Any other use of the list requires express, written permission in advance. ================================================================ How to submit update information for this list ================================================================ Updates can be sent to BOBsBBS at 916-929-7511 or on our WWW homepage at "http://www.channel1.com/usbbs/". *Minimum* requirements for NEW listings on USBBS include: (1) Modem(s) supporting 2400 bps or greater operation; (2) 100 MB of disk capacity devoted to the BBS; (3) 24hr/7 day service; and (4) Sysop must give REAL NAME in listing. The USBBS list is QUITE selective and is for BBSs that are oriented to serious users of DOS computers. These criteria are admittedly subjective and rest in the discretion of the editor of the list. Impolite complaints about these decisions will be politely ignored. ================================================================ Columns 55-57 show the number of the USBBS list on which a BBS was first listed: 06 = 11/84, 26 = 7/1/86, 55=12/1/88, 88=9/1/91, 100=9/1/92. Cols. 75-79 show the size in 100s of megs and number of nodes. For example, 1/2 would mean 100 megs, 2 nodes and 50/ would be 5 Gigs and only 1 node (the default). A + between the megs and nodes indicates CD-ROM. Col 46=Board Software, 47=Pay board indicator, 48=Internet Services (see table at end of list). Under FEATURES, cols. 75-79 show the size and number of nodes as follows: default = less than 100 megs; 1/ = 100 megs, 1 line 50/5 = 5 Gigs and 5 nodes.
